# Changelog

# üì¶ 0.11.0-beta

## üì∞ General changes and notes

Summary of changes here!

<details open>
<summary>Github Commits :octocat:</summary>
<blockquote>

- Modified Kanto League from RGS (Uncandango)
- Prevent Pokecenter to spawn on Void (Uncandango)
- Disabled other RGS gyms (Uncandango)
- Prevent relocate campfire (Uncandango)
- Removed catch restrictions until full release (Uncandango)
- Prevent Pokecenter to spawn on Nether (LobsterJonn)
- Added village gyms for both bdsp and radical red series (LobsterJonn)
- Restrict oil lakes to beaches (LobsterJonn)
- Disabled spawns for legendary, ultra beast and paradox mons added by MissingMons (LobsterJonn)
- Blacklist TM machines from relocation (LobsterJonn)
- Remove diamond from oritech overworld resource nodes (LobsterJonn)
- tag create:rose_quartz as c:gems/rose_quartz (LobsterJonn)
- Changed Bathsalts Gliscor to have poisonheal ability (LobsterJonn)
- Added wits command (LobsterJonn)
- Added Chosen and Direwolf structures (Uncandango/LobsterJonn)
- Add souns to menu and game and EnderDrive removal message (Uncandango)
- Add relocation not supported for block category (Uncandango)
- Added size variations to mons (LobsterJonn)
- Support for custom balls in Ball Launcher (LobsterJonn)
- Added config for egg incubation time (LobsterJonn)
- Fixed crash when using apricorn leaves in framed blocks and schematicanon (LobsterJonn)
- Made CobbleWorker jobs work with modded inventories (LobsterJonn)
- Exposed Gilded Chests inventory to NeoForge ItemHandler (LobsterJonn)
- Added pokemon themed music discs (Uncandango)
- Fixed some PNC recipes and lowered pressure requirement to 4.8 instead of 5 (LobsterJonn)
- Fixed genderless mons being able to breed with male mons (LobsterJonn)
- Exposed TM Machine inventory for pipe insertion (LobsterJonn)
- Disable Cobblemon pokecenters in villages (LobsterJonn)

</blockquote>

</details>

---

<details>
<summary>allthemons/pnc/chamber/brass_ancient__ball_mechanism</summary>

```diff
+{
+  type: "pneumaticcraft:pressure_chamber"
+  inputs: [
+    {
+      count: 2
+      item: "createmonballsoverhaul:brass_ball_base"
+    }
+    {
+      count: 1
+      item: "create:andesite_alloy"
+    }
+    {
+      count: 1
+      item: "create:shaft"
+    }
+  ]
+  pressure: 4
+  results: [
+    {
+      count: 1
+      id: "createmonballsoverhaul:brass_ancient_ball_mechanism"
+    }
+  ]
+}

```


</details>

<details>
<summary>apotheosis/gem_case</summary>

```diff
+{
+  type: "minecraft:crafting_shaped"
+  category: "misc"
+  group: "apotheosis"
+  key: {
+    B: {
+      item: "minecraft:basalt"
+    }
+    E: {
+      item: "apotheosis:gem_cutting_table"
+    }
+    G: {
+      tag: "c:glass_blocks"
+    }
+    N: {
+      item: "minecraft:ender_chest"
+    }
+  }
+  pattern: [
+    "GGG"
+    "BEB"
+    "BNB"
+  ]
+  result: {
+    count: 1
+    id: "apotheosis:gem_case"
+  }
+}

```


</details>

<details>
<summary>apotheosis/infusion/ender_gem_case</summary>

```diff
+{
+  type: "apothic_enchanting:keep_nbt_infusion"
+  input: {
+    item: "apotheosis:gem_case"
+  }
+  requirements: {
+    eterna: 100
+    quanta: 100
+    arcana: 45
+  }
+  max_requirements: {
+    eterna: 100
+    quanta: 100
+    arcana: 50
+  }
+  result: {
+    id: "apotheosis:ender_gem_case"
+    count: 1
+  }
+}

```

<details>
<summary>apotheosis/salvaging/other/compressed_iron_armor</summary>

```diff
+{
+  neoforge:conditions: [
+    {
+      type: "almostunified:conditional"
+      conditions_met: true
+      original_conditions: [
+        {
+          type: "neoforge:mod_loaded"
+          modid: "pneumaticcraft"
+        }
+      ]
+    }
+  ]
+  type: "apotheosis:salvaging"
+  input: [
+    {
+      item: "pneumaticcraft:compressed_iron_helmet"
+    }
+    {
+      item: "pneumaticcraft:compressed_iron_chestplate"
+    }
+    {
+      item: "pneumaticcraft:compressed_iron_leggings"
+    }
+    {
+      item: "pneumaticcraft:compressed_iron_boots"
+    }
+  ]
+  outputs: [
+    {
+      max_count: 2
+      min_count: 0
+      stack: {
+        count: 1
+        id: "minecraft:leather"
+      }
+    }
+    {
+      max_count: 3
+      min_count: 1
+      stack: {
+        count: 1
+        id: "pneumaticcraft:ingot_iron_compressed"
+      }
+    }
+  ]
+}

```

+            }
